      <script>
       fallback.ready(function () {
		$(window).load(function() {
			var userId = $.cookie('FCB_USERID_COOKIE');
           	if (userId != null && $.isNumeric(userId) && userId > 0) {
           		var userinfo = $.cookie('FCB_USERINFO_COOKIE');
        		if (userinfo != null && userinfo.length != 0) {
        			var userTime = $.cookie('FCB_USERTIME_COOKIE');
        			var userInformation = userinfo.split("@@");
        			if (userInformation != null && userInformation.length != 0 && userInformation[1] != null && userInformation[1].length != 0 && userInformation[2] != null && userInformation[2].length != 0&& userTime != null && userTime.length != 0) {
        				$("#mailSend").html($("#mailSend").html().replace("[$USER_FULLNAME$]", unescape(userInformation[1])));
        				$("#mailSend").html($("#mailSend").html().replace("[$USER_MAIL$]", unescape(userInformation[2])));
        				$("#mailSend").html($("#mailSend").html().replace("[$USER_DIFFTIME$]", userTime));
        				
        				var userVerificationTemplate = $("#userVerificationTemplate").html();
    					userVerificationTemplate = userVerificationTemplate.replace("[$USER_FULLNAME$]", unescape(userInformation[1]));
    					userVerificationTemplate = userVerificationTemplate.replace("[$USER_DIFFTIME$]", userTime);
    					
    					var userVerificationSection = $('#userVerificationSection');
    					userVerificationSection.html("");
    					userVerificationSection.append(userVerificationTemplate);
    					
    					$('.notification__close button').on('click', function () {
    						$('.notification').hide();
    					});
        			}
        		}
           	}
           	
           	var ticketKey = getUrlParameter(window.location.search, 'ticketKey');
			var passwordReset = getUrlParameter(window.location.search, 'passwordReset');
			if ((userId == null || userId == 0) && ticketKey != null && ticketKey.length != 0 && passwordReset != null && passwordReset == "true" && $('#openPasswordReset').length != 0) {
				var url = $('#openPasswordReset').data('src');
				if (url != null && url.length != 0) {
					$('#openPasswordReset').data('src', url.replace('TICKET_KEY', ticketKey));
					$('#openPasswordReset').trigger('click');
				}
			}
			
			var verificationPopup = getUrlParameter(window.location.search, 'verificationPopup');
			if (verificationPopup != null && verificationPopup == "true" && $('#verificationDialog').length != 0) {
				var userTime = $.cookie('FCB_USERTIME_COOKIE');
				if (userTime != null && userTime.length != 0) {					
					$("#mailVerification").html($("#mailVerification").html().replace("[$USER_DIFFTIME$]", userTime));
					$('#verificationDialog').trigger('click');					
					setTimeout(function(){ 
						$('#dialog').find('.button--close').on('click', function () {
							$('#dialog').find('.dialog--close-button').click();
					   	});
					}
					, 500);
				}
			}
			
			var premiumVerificationPopup = getUrlParameter(window.location.search, 'premiumVerificationPopup');
			if (premiumVerificationPopup != null && premiumVerificationPopup == "true" && $('#verificationDialogPremium').length != 0) {
				var userTime = $.cookie('FCB_USERTIME_COOKIE');
				if (userTime != null && userTime.length != 0) {
					$("#mailVerificationPremium").html($("#mailVerificationPremium").html().replace("[$USER_DIFFTIME$]", userTime));
					AUI().use('aui-base', 'aui-io-request', function(A) {
						var url = "/c/portal/cookie/info";
						A.io.request(url,{
							method: 'POST',
							data: {
								"userId": userId
								},
							on: {
								success: function() {							
									var data = JSON.parse(this.get('responseData'));
									dataLayer.push(data);
									$('#verificationDialogPremium').trigger('click');
								},
								error:function() {
									$('#verificationDialogPremium').trigger('click');
								}
							}
						});						
					});
				}
			}
			
			var facebookRegistered = getUrlParameter(window.location.search, 'facebookRegistered');
			if (facebookRegistered != null && facebookRegistered == "true" ) {
				trackEventActions('paginaVirtual', '', '', '', '/fans/facebook-registre-confirmat');
				trackEventActions('everisEvent', 'registre', 'registre', 'facebook');
			}
		});
	});
      </script>

               <script>
                fallback.ready(function () {
            $(document).ready(function() {
            	var userId = $.cookie('FCB_USERID_COOKIE');
            	if (userId != null && $.isNumeric(userId) && userId > 0) {
            		var userinfo = $.cookie('FCB_USERINFO_COOKIE');
            		if (userinfo != null && userinfo.length != 0) {
            			var userInformation = userinfo.split("@@");
            			if (userInformation != null && userInformation.length != 0 && userInformation[0] != null && userInformation[0].length != 0) {
            				var userLoggedTemplate = $("#userLoggedTemplate").html();
                			userLoggedTemplate = userLoggedTemplate.replace("[$USER_FIRSTNAME$]", unescape(userInformation[0]));
                			
                			var userSection = $('#userSection');
                			userSection.html("");
                			userSection.append(userLoggedTemplate);

    						FCB.secondaryMenu.init();
    						FCB.dialog.init();
            			}
            		}
            	}
            	
            	var loginPopupAjax = getUrlParameter(window.location.search, 'loginPopup');
				if (loginPopupAjax != null && loginPopupAjax == "true") {
					openLoginWindow();
				}
                                   
				var registerPopupAjax = getUrlParameter(window.location.search, 'registerPopup');
				if (registerPopupAjax != null && registerPopupAjax == "true") {
					openPremiumRegister();
				}
			});
		});
               </script>
